MOD_NAME=SQUADRON UNLEASHED 
AUTHOR=szmind
DESCRIPTION=This is a heavy mod - expect c.a. 30s of applying it by PatcherGUI. Enables squadron interceptions in place of single-jet dodge fights, allows for sending partially damaged ships, redefines stance mechanics allowing for quasi-formation management, makes pilot rank mean more than a badge and some more. Most key parameters can be tuned to player's preference and also effectively turn off certain features. Study and edit "ALIAS=..." lines just below for that purpose. Keeping a backup of modifed UPK files is advised - PatcherGUI will make the backups, so just keep them.

//Let's go :)

/***********************************************************************************************************
THIS IS  CONFIGURATION SECTION. YOU CAN FREELY CHANGE MANY PARAMETERS RELATED TO AIRCOMBAT IN GENERAL
AND THIS MOD PARTICULARLY. YOU MIGHT FIND STH YOU ALWAYS WANTED TO CHANGE RIGHT FROM SCRATCH :)
YOU CAN ALSO SKIP IT FOR NOW AND USE A SEPARATE, MUCH QUICKER 'CONFIGURATOR' LATER
**********************************************************************************************************/
UPK_FILE=xcomstrategygame.upk 

//----------------------------------------------- 
//SHIP SELECTION AND LITTLE COLOR MANAGEMENT
// For alternative color codes see end of config section
//-----------------------------------------------
ALIAS=MinHP_PctToLaunch:<%f 0.50>		// if a jet has minimum that fraction of HP it can be launched
ALIAS=MinSquadronSize:<%b 1>			//self explanatory
ALIAS=MaxSquadronSize:<%b 6>			//self explanatory
ALIAS=DamagedJetSpeedModifier:<%f 0.8>	//if you launch a damaged jet, its geoscape/engagement speed will be multiplied by this factor; default 0.80 
ALIAS=DamagedJetAimPenalty:<%i 25>		// if you are sending a damaged jet it will suffer that much of penalty to aim
ALIAS=AggroLabelColor:04 				//color of label for selected 'good' ships; default 04 (yellow)
ALIAS=AggroDamagedColor:0A			// color of label for selected 'damaged' ships; default 0A (orange)
ALIAS=HeaderSelectedColor:07 			// color of name/weapon labels for selected 'good' ships; default 07 (cyan)
ALIAS=EngageWeaponStringFontSize:<%b 18>	//set font size of weapon label on the engagement screen
ALIAS=EngageWeaponStringColorNormal:05 	//set normal color of weapon label on the engagement screen; default 05 (white)
ALIAS=EngageWeaponStringColorDamaged:0C 	//set color of damaged ship weapon label on the engagement screen; default 0C (orange)
ALIAS=EngageHPBarColor:07			//default: cyan (07), standard game's color :)
//----------------------------------------------- 
//'UFO Interception Tweak' mod incorporation; 
// with permission of SpazmoJones (aka Eclipse666) and with credit to him
//-----------------------------------------------
ALIAS=SpazmoFactor:<%f 1.0>		//time MULTIPLIER/damage DIVISOR (don't you dare setting zero :) from "UFO Interception Tweak" by SpazmoJones (here default at 1.0)
ALIAS=SloMoPlayback:<%f 1.0>	//you can slow down time passing during engagement with this; set it < 1.0 (or speed up > 1.0)
//------------------------------------------------
// COMBAT MECHANICS RELATED STAFF
//------------------------------------------------
ALIAS=PenaltyToHitSmallUFO:<%b 10>		//shots at small-sized UFOs suffer that much of penalty to aim
ALIAS=BonusToHitLargeUFO:<%b 15>		//shots at large-sized UFOs have that much of bonus to aim
ALIAS=AGG_JetVulnerability:<%f 1.25>		//damage received by AGG jet is multiplied by this factor
ALIAS=SpeedBoostForDEFUFO:<%f 1.50> 		//battle speed of DEF UFO is multiplied by this
ALIAS=SpeedDownForAGGUFO:<%f 0.50>		//battle speed of AGG UFO is multiplied by this
ALIAS=CooldownModForAGGUFO:<%f 0.50>	//UFO weapons' cooldown on AGG is multiplied by this
ALIAS=AGG_AimBonus:<%b 15>			//this is added to chance to hit for ships with AGG stance
ALIAS=DEF_AimPenalty:<%b 15>		//this is subtracted from chance to hit for ships with DEF stance
ALIAS=DEFHitToMiss:1D <%i 20>			//percent chance to turn hit at DEF jet into miss ("dodge"). Default 20.
ALIAS=AimBonusPerKill:<%i 3>			// this is added to interceptor's chance to hit; per each kill
ALIAS=MaxBonusForKills:<%i 30>			// no more aim bonus for kills above this number
ALIAS=BAL_SupportHitRisk:1D <%i 20>		//percent chance for supporting ship on BAL to be hit by "lone bullet". Default 20
ALIAS=AGG_SupportHitRisk:1D <%i 40>		//percent chance for supporting ship on AGG to be hit by "lone bullet". Default 40
ALIAS=LoneBulletDamageScaler:1E <%f 0.8>	// damage dealt by 'lone bullets' will be multiplied by this factor (float). Default 1.0
ALIAS=AutoAbortThreshold:1E <%f 0.25>		//fraction of HP at which supporting ship auto-disengages; 0.0 results in 'never abort'. Default 0.25
ALIAS=CritMaxChance:1D <%i 25>			//max % chance for crit hit
ALIAS=CritMinChance:1D <%i 5>			//min % chance for crit hit
ALIAS=CritDamageMultiplier:1E <%f 1.5>		// crit damage = normal damage x this factor
ALIAS=SparrowhawkDamageDivisor:<%f 0.50> 	//Sparrowhawks damage is of stingray's multiplied by this
ALIAS=UFODestructionChanceScaler:<%f 1.0>	// fraction of original LW destruction chance, e.g. 0.75 would mean 75% of orig LW chance
ALIAS=UFODestructionPctThreshold:<%b 10>	// that much initial destruction chance is ignored resulting in auto-crash
/************************************************
UFO destruction modifiers. You can scale original LW chance of UFO destruction with one simple factor.
This still means that even a small overkill translates into small chance of destruction.
Therefore you can also set a minimum threshold of overkill above which the chance starts occuring at all.
The threshold translates into percent chance that must be accumulated before it is applied at all.
So for example setting threshold at 20 means that if chance of destruction is < 20% UFO crashes without checking the chance.
Well, actually the check is performed but you get a +20 handicap (your dice rolls 20-120 instead of 0-100)
If you overkill for 30% chance with the above setting the actual chance will be (30 - 20)= 10%
**********************************************/
/*---------------------------------------------------------
						Alternative color codes 
						01  - Grey
						02  - Green (original)
						03  - Red
						04  - Yellow
						05  - White
						06  - Green (original)
						07	- Cyan (basic)
						08	- Cyan
						09	- Cyan
						0A  - Orange
						0B  - Purple
						0C  - Orange
						other  - Cyan
--------------------------------------------------------*/

MODDING PART STARTS HERE. IF YOU ARE A MOD DEVELOPER OR WISH TO BECOME ONE YOU MAY CONTINUE STUDYING.
OTHERWISE THERE IS PROBABLY NOTHING MORE OF INTEREST TO YOU.
**********************************************************************************************************

NEW TABLE ENTRIES - THESE WILL NOT BE UNINSTALLED WITH PATCHERGUI (BUT IT IS NO HARM); only via XComStrategyGame.UPK backup file
I exclude this section from uninstall cause it does not uninstall properly - not buggy, but it would leave some garbage 
like @NULL displayed with UE Explorer in the 'owner' objects.
*******************************************************************************/
UNINSTALL=FALSE

//------------------------------------------------------------------------
//ADDING iSquadronSize LOCAL VARIABLE TO ToggleInterceptor FUNCTION
//-------------------------------------------------------------------------

[ADD_NAME_ENTRY]
	<%u14>           		// name length (including terminating null)
	<%t"iSquadronSize">  	// variable name
	<%u0x00000000>  		// flags L 
	<%u0x00070010>  		// flags H 

[ADD_EXPORT_ENTRY]
	<Core.IntProperty> 		// Type
	<NullRef>          		// ParentClassRef
	<XGInterception.ToggleInterceptor>  // OwnerRef
	<iSquadronSize>         // NameIdx
	<NullRef>   	// ArchetypeRef
	<%u0x00000000>  // flags H
	<%u0x00070004>  // flags L
	<%u40>          // serial size
	<%u0>           // serial offset
	<%u0>           // export flags
	<%u0>           // net objects count
	<%u0>           // GUID1, zero if net objects count == 0
	<%u0>           // GUID2, zero if net objects count == 0
	<%u0>           // GUID3, zero if net objects count == 0
	<%u0>           // GUID4, zero if net objects count == 0
	<%u0>           // unknown, zero if net objects count == 0

OBJECT=XGInterception.ToggleInterceptor.iSquadronSize
REL_OFFSET=16   // skip PrevObjRef + Empty DefaultProperties List + NextObjRef
[MODDED_CODE]
	<%s1>		    // ArrayDim
	<%s0>		    // ElementSize
	<%u0>  			// flags L
	<%u0>  			// flags H
	<None>  		// CategoryIndex part
	<NullRef>  		// ArrayEnumRef

//----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//I USE "m_kTShip.iRange" REFERENCE FREQUENTLY IN THIS MOD, WHILE GetRange() IS USED NOWHERE
//IN ORIGINAL GAME (INCLUDING LONG WAR). SO I TWEAK IT TO SIMPLY RETURN m_kTShip.iRange 
//AND MAKE USE OF IT IN LATER CODE.
//----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

OBJECT=XGShip.GetRange
/*---this one in pure hex cause whole function is just one line :)-----*/
[BEFORE_HEX]
04 //return
	90 //multiply; being removed
		35 //structure member token
			72 25 00 00 //XGStrategyActorNativBase.TShip.iRange (member ref)
			7B 25 00 00 //XGStrategyActorNativBase.TShip (structure ref)
			00 00 //byte
			01 48 4B 00 00 // m_kTShip (expression to the left of ".Range")
		2C 64 // 100; this will be removed
	16 // end parameter token closing 90(multiply); to be removed

[AFTER_HEX]
04 //return
	35 //structure member token
		72 25 00 00 //XGStrategyActorNativBase.TShip.iRange
		7B 25 00 00 //XGStrategyActorNativBase.TShip
		00 00 //byte
		01 48 4B 00 00 // m_kTShip
		0B 0B 0B 0B //filler code replacing removed bytes to match original size

/***********************************************************************
SETTING UFO STANCE RANDOMLY ON UFO DETECTION
***********************************************************************/
OBJECT = XGGeoscape.OnUFODetected : AUTO
[REPLACEMENT_CODE]
/*(0x0000/0x0000)*/ 0F 00 <.kUFO> 19 1B <AI> 16 [@] <XGStrategyAI.GetUFO.ReturnValue> 00 ( 1B <GetUFO> 00 <.iUFO> 16 ) 
/*(0x0033/0x0027)*/ 0F 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip_UFO.m_iCounter> 00 ( 01 <XGShip_UFO.m_iCounter> ) A3 01 <@m_iDetectedUFOs> 16 
/*(0x005D/0x0041)*/ 07 [@label_0x00BB] 9A 38 3A 35 <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TShip.eType> <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TShip> 00 00 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip.m_kTShip> 00 ( 01 <XGShip.m_kTShip> ) 38 3A 24 09 16 
/*(0x0099/0x0069)*/ 	14 19 1B <HQ> 16 [@] <XGHeadQuarters.m_bHyperwaveActivated> 00 ( 2D 01 <XGHeadQuarters.m_bHyperwaveActivated> ) 27 
						
						//SET m_iSTATUS TO 1; SO THAT OVERSEER STAYS ON BAL
						0F 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip.m_iStatus> 00 ( 01 <XGShip.m_iStatus> ) 26
/*(0x00BB/0x0083)*/ [#label_0x00BB]

					//CHECK IF UFO HAS THE STANCE ALREADY SET, AND IF NOT SET IT (RANDOM)
					//if(kUFO.m_iStatus == 0);
					07 [@MakeAlert] 9A 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip.m_iStatus> 00 ( 01 <XGShip.m_iStatus> ) 25 16
						
							//kUFO.m_kTShip.iRange = Rand(3);
							0F 35 <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TShip.iRange> <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TShip> 00 00 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip.m_kTShip> 00 ( 01 <XGShip.m_kTShip> ) 
							1C <Core.Object.Rand> 2C 03 16 
						
						[#StanceSet]
						//CHANGE UFO STATUS TO 1 MARKING IT: 'STANCE SET'
						//kUFOt.m_iStatus = 1
						0F 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip.m_iStatus> 00 ( 01 <XGShip.m_iStatus> ) 26
										
					[#MakeAlert]
/*(0x00BB/0x0083)*/ 07 [@label_0x0174] 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip.IsFlying.ReturnValue> 00 ( 1B <IsFlying> 16 ) 
/*(0x00DD/0x009D)*/ 	1B <Alert> 1B <MakeAlert> 24 00 00 <.iUFO> 4A 4A 4A 16 16 
/*(0x00FF/0x00BB)*/ 	07 [@label_0x0171] 9A 35 <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TObjective.eType> <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TObjective> 00 00 19 19 00 <.kUFO> [@] <XGShip_UFO.m_kObjective> 00 ( 01 <XGShip_UFO.m_kObjective> ) [@] <XGAlienObjective.m_kTObjective> 00 ( 01 <XGAlienObjective.m_kTObjective> ) 24 09 16 
/*(0x014C/0x00EC)*/ 		19 1B <PRES> 16 [@] <NullRef> 00 ( 1B <Notify> 2C 34 4A 4A 4A 16 ) 
/*(0x0171/0x010D)*/ 	[#label_0x0171]
/*(0x0171/0x010D)*/ 	06 [@label_0x0216]

/*---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Adding here a block of code to pre-calculate aggro stat and sort the akIntDistance array
The array holds interceptors on the continent together with a spare iMiles stat. 
I am calculating Aggro based on XGInterceptionEngagement.Init formulas:
2 x WeaponLevel +1 for Firestorm. 
I am adding Cannon = 7 (lvl 1 weapon), +2 for AGG stance, -2 for DEF stance.
I use iIndex as temporary storage for aggro value. I will use iMiles as storage place 
for calculated aggro stat and then use a ready function XGInterceptionUI.IntDistanceSort 
which sorts akIntDistance based on iMiles stat - effectively will it sort the array based on aggro.
We need an iterator to cycle through the array so I will use iJet which is a spare one for now.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

/*CALCULATE AND UPDATE EXPECTED TimeUntilOutrun BASED ON SLOWEST JET IN SQUADRON VS UFO SPEED
I will use kTag.IntValue0 and kTag.IntValue1 as temporary 'locals' (iterator / speed storage).
Finally I will store calculated time in m_kTarget.txtSpeed.StrValue (which is not used anywhere).
Then I will call it from within UFORadarContactAlert.UpdateData.
I am using 'I', 'Speed' and 'UFOSpeed' aliases defined at top.

I = 0;
Speed = 999;
Next:
if(I < m_kInterception.m_arrInterceptors.Length)
[	
	if(m_kInterception.m_arrInterceptors[I].IsDamaged()
		Speed = Min(Speed, <DamagedJetSpeedModifier> * m_kInterception.m_arrInterceptors[I].m_kTShip.iEngagementSpeed);
	else
		Speed = Min(Speed, m_kInterception.m_arrInterceptors[I].m_kTShip.iEngagementSpeed);
	++I;
	goto Next;
]
if(m_kUFO.GetRange()) == 0)
	UFOSpeed = m_kUFO.m_kTShip.iEngagementSpeed
else
	UFOSpeed = m_kUFO.m_kTShip.iEngagementSpeed * (m_kUFO.GetRange() == 1 ? <SpeedDownForAGGUFO> : <SpeedBoostForDEFUFO> ) 

m_kTarget.txtSpeed.StrValue = Left(string(<SpazmoFactor> * 30.0 * Speed / UFOSpeed); 4)


-------------AND INTO PSEUDO:
*/
0F <!I> 25

// !!!!!!!!!!!!!THIS IS TRUE HEART OF COMBAT MECHANICS!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!

OBJECT = UIInterceptionEngagement.Playback : AUTO

/***************************** 
This is a key function handling multijet fight. Basically all shots to be proceeded have been already recorded in GetCombat() function. Each shot is recorded in a separate CombatExchange ('CombEx' as I call it) marked as either UFOExchange or InterceptorExchange. A CombEx stores the following values: iSourceShip, iTargetShip, bHit, iDamage, iWeapon (not a type but 0 for main weapon and 1 for secondary weapon). In fact iTargetShip equals 1 for every UFOExchange and 0 for every InterceptorExchange. Therefore UFO shots are always applied to Interceptor No1. This iTargetShip=1 must be now updated real-time to actual index of target jet. Also crit hit and crit damage of ALL jets has been calculated with Armor of first jet. It is OK for jets of the same type. However for ships of different type this must be recalculated. 

Moreover interface is (at least for now) designed to show any damage done to player ships and apply it to the HP icon. So damage done to supporting ships is shown on the icon of leader. This is wrong, therefore I am cheating interface by telling it that bullets that hit a supporter deal 1 damage (just to show explosion but 1 damage is barely seen on the icon). Another cheat is to prevent removal of jet's image when the first ship is destroyed. So if first leader is destroyed I set its HP to 1. This cheat will be reverted in OnEngagementOver function. 

To mark ships that have aborted or are destroyed I use the iRange attribute (the same as used for stance); I am setting it to 3 (0 is BAL, 1 is AGG, 2 is DEF)

I will also have to mark somehow the 'killing shot' for proper determining salvage on shot down with EMP Cannon.
***************************/
ALIAS=CurrentUFOTarget:19 19 01 <@m_kMgr> [@] <XGInterceptionEngagementUI.m_kInterceptionEngagement> 00 ( 01 <XGInterceptionEngagementUI.m_kInterceptionEngagement> ) [@] <XGInterceptionEngagement.m_iUFOTarget> 00 ( 01 <XGInterceptionEngagement.m_iUFOTarget> )
ALIAS=TargetShipID:35 <UIInterceptionEngagement.TAttack.iTargetShip> <@TAttack> 00 01 00 <.kAttack>
ALIAS=IntEngagement:19 01 <@m_kMgr> [@] <XGInterceptionEngagementUI.m_kInterceptionEngagement> 00 ( 01 <XGInterceptionEngagementUI.m_kInterceptionEngagement> )
ALIAS=SourceShipID:35 <UIInterceptionEngagement.TAttack.iSourceShip> <@TAttack> 00 01 00 <.kAttack>
ALIAS=ArrayOfJets:19 01 <@m_kXGInterception> [@] <XGInterception.m_arrInterceptors> 00 ( 01 <XGInterception.m_arrInterceptors> )
ALIAS=kWeapon:19 00 <.kShip> [@] <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.SHIPWEAPON.ReturnValue> 00 ( 1B <SHIPWEAPON> 10 35 <XGInterceptionEngagement.CombatExchange.iWeapon> <XGInterceptionEngagement.CombatExchange> 00 00 00 <.kCombatExchange> 35 <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TShip.arrWeapons> <XGStrategyActorNativeBase.TShip> 00 01 19 00 <.kShip> [@] <XGShip.m_kTShip> 00 ( 01 <XGShip.m_kTShip> ) 16 )
ALIAS=kCombExTargetShip:10 93 35 <XGInterceptionEngagement.CombatExchange.iTargetShip> <XGInterceptionEngagement.CombatExchange> 00 00 00 <.kCombatExchange> 26 16 19 01 <@m_kXGInterception> [@] <XGInterception.m_arrInterceptors> 00 ( 01 <XGInterception.m_arrInterceptors> )

// Damage done by UFO, which is stored in CombEx, has been calculated based on first jet's armor.

// Therefore we need to check if the type is different and if so, recalculate the damage.

//
//		new damage = [old damage] x [new base damage] / [old base damage]
//
